      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span id="Lord.27s_Prayer">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lord's_Prayer">
        <a href="/wiki/Lord%27s_Prayer" title="Lord's Prayer">
         Lord's Prayer
        </a>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Asturian_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Lord's Prayer">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <table class="wikitable">
       <tr>
        <th>
         Asturian
        </th>
        <th>
         Galician
        </th>
        <th>
         Latin
        </th>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         <p>
          Pá nuesu que tas nel cielu, santificáu seya'l to nome. Amiye'l to reinu, fágase la to voluntá, lo mesmo na tierra que'n cielu. El nuesu pan de tolos díes dánoslu güei ya perdónanos les nueses ofenses, lo mesmo que nós facemos colos que nos faltaron. Nun nos dexes cayer na tentación, ya llíbranos del mal. Amén.
         </p>
        </td>
        <td>
         <p>
          Noso Pai que estás no ceo: santificado sexa o teu nome, veña a nós o teu reino e fágase a túa vontade aquí na terra coma no ceo. O noso pan de cada día dánolo hoxe; e perdóanos as nosas ofensas como tamén perdoamos nós a quen nos ten ofendido; e non nos deixes caer na tentación, mais líbranos do mal. Amén.
         </p>
        </td>
        <td>
         <p>
          Pater noster, qui es in caelis, Sanctificetur nomen tuum. Adveniat regnum tuum. Fiat voluntas tua, Sicut in caelo et in terra. Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie. Et dimitte nobis debita nostra, Sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris. Et ne nos inducas in tentationem: Sed libera nos a malo. Amen
         </p>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Education">
        Education
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Asturian_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Education">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Primary_and_secondary">
        Primary and secondary
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Asturian_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Primary and secondary">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Although Spanish is the official language of all schools in Asturias, in many schools children are allowed to take Asturian-language classes from age 6 to 16. Elective classes are also offered from 16 to 19. Central Asturias (
       <a href="/wiki/Nal%C3%B3n_(comarca)" title="Nalón (comarca)">
        Nalón
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Caudal_(comarca)" title="Caudal (comarca)">
        Caudal
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Comarcas_of_Asturias" title="Comarcas of Asturias">
        comarcas
       </a>
       ) has the largest percentage of Asturian-language students, with almost 80 percent of primary-school students and 30 percent of secondary-school students in Asturian classes.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">
        <a href="#cite_note-33">
         [33]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <a href="/wiki/Gij%C3%B3n_(comarca)" title="Gijón (comarca)">
        Xixón
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Oviedo_(comarca)" title="Oviedo (comarca)">
        Uviéu
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Eo-Navia_(comarca)" title="Eo-Navia (comarca)">
        Eo-Navia
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Oriente_(comarca)" title="Oriente (comarca)">
        Oriente
       </a>
       also have an increased number of students.
      </p>
      <div class="thumb noresize tnone" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right:auto; overflow:hidden; width:auto; max-width:758px;">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="">
        <div class="overflowbugx" style="overflow:auto;">
         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Schooling_asturian_language.png" title="Development of Asturian-language education">
          <img alt="Blue-and-red bar graph" data-file-height="528" data-file-width="1141" height="347" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Schooling_asturian_language.png/750px-Schooling_asturian_language.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Schooling_asturian_language.png/1125px-Schooling_asturian_language.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/23/Schooling_asturian_language.png 2x" width="750"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Schooling_asturian_language.png" title="File:Schooling asturian language.png">
          </a>
         </div>
         Development of Asturian-language education
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">
          <a href="#cite_note-34">
           [34]
          </a>
         </sup>
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">
          <a href="#cite_note-35">
           [35]
          </a>
         </sup>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="University">
        University
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Asturian_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: University">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       According to article six of the
       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Oviedo" title="University of Oviedo">
        University of Oviedo
       </a>
       charter, "The University of Oviedo, due to its historical, social and economic links with the Principality of Asturias, will devote particular attention to the cultural aspects and collective interests of Asturias. The Asturian Language will be treated appropriately in accordance with legislation. Nobody will be discriminated against for using it".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">
        <a href="#cite_note-36">
         [36]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Asturian can be used at the university in accordance with the Use of Asturian Act. University records indicate an increased number of courses and amount of scientific work using Asturian, with courses in the Department of Philology and Educational Sciences.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">
        <a href="#cite_note-37">
         [37]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In accordance with the
       <a href="/wiki/Bologna_Process" title="Bologna Process">
        Bologna Process
       </a>
       , Asturian
       <a href="/wiki/Philology" title="Philology">
        philology
       </a>
       will be available for study and teachers will be able to specialise in the Asturian language at the University of Oviedo.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Internet">
        Internet
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Asturian_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Internet">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Asturian government websites,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">
        <a href="#cite_note-38">
         [38]
        </a>
       </sup>
       council webpages, blogs,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">
        <a href="#cite_note-39">
         [39]
        </a>
       </sup>
       entertainment webpages and social networks exist.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">
        <a href="#cite_note-40">
         [40]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <a href="/wiki/Free_software" title="Free software">
        Free software
       </a>
       is offered in Asturian, and
       <a href="/wiki/Ubuntu_(operating_system)" title="Ubuntu (operating system)">
        Ubuntu
       </a>
       offers Asturian as an operating-system language.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">
        <a href="#cite_note-41">
         [41]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
        <a href="#cite_note-42">
         [42]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Free software in the language is available from
       <a href="/wiki/Debian" title="Debian">
        Debian
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Fedora" title="Fedora">
        Fedora
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Firefox" title="Firefox">
        Firefox
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Mozilla_Thunderbird" title="Mozilla Thunderbird">
        Thunderbird
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/LibreOffice" title="LibreOffice">
        LibreOffice
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/VLC_media_player" title="VLC media player">
        VLC
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/GNOME" title="GNOME">
        GNOME
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Chromium" title="Chromium">
        Chromium
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/KDE" title="KDE">
        KDE
       </a>
       .
      </p>

        <li id="cite_note-19">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-19">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          <a class="external free" href="http://www.grufia.com/Ficheros/Fuero%20de%20Aviles.pdf" rel="nofollow">
           http://www.grufia.com/Ficheros/Fuero%20de%20Aviles.pdf
          </a>
         </span>
        </li>
        <li id="cite_note-20">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-20">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          <a class="external text" href="http://revistadeliteratura.revistas.csic.es/index.php/revistadeliteratura/article/download/188/199" rel="nofollow">
           Los refranes o proverbios en Romance, Hernán Nuñez, pag 12
          </a>
          This document has got a unique reference, supposedly in Asturian: "
          <i>
           Quien passa por Ruycande y no bebe, o muere de hambre, o no ha sede
          </i>
          " Who passes through Ruycande Village and do not drink, or starves or don not have thirst", Hernán Nunez, Refranes o Proverbios en romance que coligio y gloso el comenadador Hernán Nunez, professor de retorica y griego en la Universidad de Salamanca, Lerida, año 1621, p. 81.
         </span>
        </li>
        <li id="cite_note-21">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-21">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          About the character of this literature the Swedish philologist
          <a class="extiw" href="https://sv.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C3%85ke_Munthe" title="sv:Åke Munthe">
           Åke W:son Munthe
          </a>
          on 1868 notes the following:
          <i>
           "it seems to subsist in this literature an arbitrary mixture of Castilian language elements. This literary production -after a long century of copy and paste and finally because of the editor's final review- seems to be shown in nowadays in a very confusing way. For that reason, we must appoint to Reguera as the author of this literature, that I could call 'bable'. All the later authors, at least from a linguistic point of view, all of them come from his literature archaizing. Naturally, some of these authors take elements of their respective local dialects, and often, also, with others languages, that in some way or another, could have got in contact, as well as of a Spanish language mixture, affected by the 'bable' or not. This literature in 'bable' cannot be considered as a literary language, because have not got any unified body, at least from a linguistic point of view... what in any case, as in whatever other dialects, seems doomed to extinction"
          </i>
          . Ake W:son Munthe,
          <i>
           Anotaciones sobre el habla popular del occidente de Asturias
          </i>
          Upsala 1887, reedition, Publisher Service of the Oviedo University, 1987, p. 3.
         </span>
        </li>

          <a class="external free" href="http://directo.uniovi.es/catalogo/FichaAsignatura.asp?asignatura=2123" rel="nofollow">
           http://directo.uniovi.es/catalogo/FichaAsignatura.asp?asignatura=2123
          </a>
          <a class="external free" href="http://directo.uniovi.es/catalogo/FichaAsignatura.asp?asignatura=2123" rel="nofollow">
           http://directo.uniovi.es/catalogo/FichaAsignatura.asp?asignatura=2123
          </a>
          , Conocimiento global de la realidad la lengua asturiana, de su unidad e independencia al margen de los fenómenos de variación interna y de su integración en el marco hispano-románico, a partir de un enfoque esencialmente histórico y diacrónico.
         </span>
        </li>
        <li id="cite_note-38">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-38">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          <a class="external text" href="http://www.asturias.es/portal/site/webasturias/menuitem.91cd0facbcdb17a73e2d6f77f2300030/?vgnextoid=d3f56fc85c97d210VgnVCM1000002f030003RCRD&amp;i18n.http.lang=ast" rel="nofollow">
           Government of the Principality of Asturias – Official Website
          </a>
         </span>
        </li>
        <li id="cite_note-39">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-39">

           </a>
          </b>
         </span>

          <a class="external text" href="http://www.asturies.com/canalblogues" rel="nofollow">
           Blog Channel in Asturian language
          </a>
         </span>
        </li>
        <li id="cite_note-40">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">

           </a>
